  .linkify {
    display: inline;
    padding: 0;
    margin: 0;

    color: var(--chops-link-color);

  }
  a:hover, .linkify:hover {
    text-decoration: underline;

  a.button, .button {
    /* Links that look like buttons. */

    text-decoration: none;

  textarea, select, input {
    box-sizing: border-box;

  }
  /* Note: decoupling heading levels from styles is useful for
  * accessibility because styles will not always line up with semantically

        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;

        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>

        <p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

On Chrome on Android after patch



<span class="line"><!---->On Chrome on Android after patch<!----></span>





 



<span class="line"><!----> <!----></span>





crrev.com/c/3990410



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/c/3990410"><!---->crrev.com/c/3990410<!----></a>





 the fullscreen notification toast is now displayed in bottom instead of top position, if shown in the bottom position I found that Android keyboard able to overlap fullscreen notification toast, so user will not see the fullscreen toast.



<span class="line"><!----> the fullscreen notification toast is now displayed in bottom instead of top position, if shown in the bottom position I found that Android keyboard able to overlap fullscreen notification toast, so user will not see the fullscreen toast.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





- Chrome Dev 109.0.5394.4 on Android 13; Android Emulator; Pixel_2_API_33 



<span class="line"><!---->- Chrome Dev 109.0.5394.4 on Android 13; Android Emulator; Pixel_2_API_33 <!----></span>



<br>





- Chrome Dev 109.0.5394.3 on Android 11; Mi 9T



<span class="line"><!---->- Chrome Dev 109.0.5394.3 on Android 11; Mi 9T<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





1. Visit attached testcase-spoof.html



<span class="line"><!---->1. Visit attached testcase-spoof.html<!----></span>



<br>





2. Tap "requestFullscreen" button



<span class="line"><!---->2. Tap "requestFullscreen" button<!----></span>



<br>





3. Fullscreen notification toast overlapped by Android Keyboard



<span class="line"><!---->3. Fullscreen notification toast overlapped by Android Keyboard<!----></span>

> Will see if I can suppress the OSK when entering fullscreen, but there might be a hack to work around it again.



<span class="line"><!---->&gt; Will see if I can suppress the OSK when entering fullscreen, but there might be a hack to work around it again.<!----></span>

I think dismissing the keyboard / temporarily suppressing is reasonable, although not sure if there are valid cases for this.



<span class="line"><!---->I think dismissing the keyboard / temporarily suppressing is reasonable, although not sure if there are valid cases for this.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





Jinsuk, given the number of security issues introduced with switching to a custom View instead of a system Toast, I wonder if need to explore different solutions. For example, we'd talked about using OS level Toast but adding rate limiting in Chrome to ensure that e.g. copy toasts didn't DoS fullscreen toasts.



<span class="line"><!---->Jinsuk, given the number of security issues introduced with switching to a custom View instead of a system Toast, I wonder if need to explore different solutions. For example, we'd talked about using OS level Toast but adding rate limiting in Chrome to ensure that e.g. copy toasts didn't DoS fullscreen toasts.<!----></span>

1. We care about the nav bar when there's no keyboard only, right? i.e. not when the keyboard is present (attached screenshot fs-k03.png).

The issue comes from the non-zero offset of Window. On most devices it is zero but for devices like Pixel 6A (or 7), it is a positive value that takes the front camera y position into account. The right way to get the bottom margin[1] is to use |bounds.height()|, not |bounds.bottom|.  



<span class="line"><!---->The issue comes from the non-zero offset of Window. On most devices it is zero but for devices like Pixel 6A (or 7), it is a positive value that takes the front camera y position into account. The right way to get the bottom margin[1] is to use |bounds.height()|, not |bounds.bottom|.  <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





        public void onGlobalLayout() {



<span class="line"><!---->        public void onGlobalLayout() {<!----></span>



<br>





            if (mContentViewInFullscreen == null || mNotificationToast == null) return;



<span class="line"><!---->            if (mContentViewInFullscreen == null || mNotificationToast == null) return;<!----></span>



<br>





            Rect bounds = new Rect();



<span class="line"><!---->            Rect bounds = new Rect();<!----></span>



<br>





            mContentViewInFullscreen.getWindowVisibleDisplayFrame(bounds);



<span class="line"><!---->            mContentViewInFullscreen.getWindowVisibleDisplayFrame(bounds);<!----></span>



<br>





            var lp = (ViewGroup.MarginLayoutParams) mNotificationToast.getLayoutParams();



<span class="line"><!---->            var lp = (ViewGroup.MarginLayoutParams) mNotificationToast.getLayoutParams();<!----></span>



<br>





            int bottomMargin = mContentViewInFullscreen.getHeight() - bounds.bottom;  <----------------



<span class="line"><!---->            int bottomMargin = mContentViewInFullscreen.getHeight() - bounds.bottom;  &lt;----------------<!----></span>



<br>





            // If positioned at the bottom of the display, shift it up to avoid overlapping



<span class="line"><!---->            // If positioned at the bottom of the display, shift it up to avoid overlapping<!----></span>



<br>





            // with the bottom nav bar when it appears by user gestures.



<span class="line"><!---->            // with the bottom nav bar when it appears by user gestures.<!----></span>



<br>





            if (bottomMargin == 0) bottomMargin = mNavbarHeight;



<span class="line"><!---->            if (bottomMargin == 0) bottomMargin = mNavbarHeight;<!----></span>



<br>





            lp.setMargins(0, 0, 0, bottomMargin);



<span class="line"><!---->            lp.setMargins(0, 0, 0, bottomMargin);<!----></span>



<br>





            mNotificationToast.requestLayout();



<span class="line"><!---->            mNotificationToast.requestLayout();<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.
